关键证据

Attacker identity: lucy
Victim object value: lili
Victim URL: http://127.0.0.1:8765/vul/overpermission/op1/op1_mem.php?username=lili&submit=submit
attacker_own_object: status=200, length=33820, sensitive_markers=role,token,permission,logout, denied=False
attacker_victim_object: status=200, length=33820, sensitive_markers=role,token,permission,logout, denied=False

复现步骤

  1. Replay the protected request to http://127.0.0.1:8765/vul/overpermission/op1/op1_mem.php?username=lucy&submit=submit across multiple identities.
  2. Mutate identifier parameter username across object boundaries.
  3. Compare status codes and sensitive response markers across identities.

修复建议

Bind object access to the authenticated subject and enforce object-level authorization for every profile/account lookup.

Status: 200
Authenticated markers: 欢迎, logout

复现步骤

  1. Open the login page http://127.0.0.1:8765/vul/xss/xsspost/post_login.php.
  2. Submit the POST login form to http://127.0.0.1:8765/vul/xss/xsspost/post_login.php.
  3. Use username=admin with the recorded masked weak/default password candidate.
  4. Confirm authenticated response markers such as logout/profile/dashboard or a post-login URL.

修复建议

Disable default credentials, require password rotation, and add rate limiting/lockout on login endpoints.
